Video (Ad) Rush

 

AOL has lots of videos and the company wants them everywhere. According to AllThingsD, video-recommendation firm -- or do you say content-marketing firm? -- Taboola and AOL have partnered to disseminate video content (and, ultimately, ads) on publisher sites, through a recommended-videos "matrix" at the bottom of stories. Half of the videos will be from AOL and the other half will be links that have traffic referral deals with Taboola. Ch-ching. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5fkjsBG1spjTfGCDeUMKGgL9gKZrzhW5PzcwnHbBKxXp162jQhYJm2jCQBrQBPaBTXcQAWdaHO89zqbPD4jICWaF9eraOwLl684ULxSNru-CHNGlHAOqTI_XmnUuVlfjZOrbQf3hMqTw4qzpdt5_xQ9ihL8avobFU2rrWCEdjhIGFEomtESAHCGn97Gj-MCLuiKQv3IZzXvf0J4Et7zOl5uGMgaQ-a7ap8wrjQ3duyMcw==> .

 

Diving At Mobile

 

Sell-side platform Rubicon Project is climbing aboard the mobile freight train, announcing on Wednesday that it has launched its own private marketplace/exchange solution for the mobile channel known as Connect. Read the release. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5dZcZryVEuLF4yT-v0jp7D6-rx9ylZcLku-2Mwn00BlO0o7R49MRy3HXdM2Ywse8LsVdrkbDzKgqJnRKxSXqzXGEHXbXKOqn3e_HXZuBklK058Fo07mBL_XdGoj_kU-L_OGDB98qOxXa7gLKEc-WNial4pGTJrIFZecSxRIE_87IsfRvewJLEcIpKVJ1bgoN27U-Q8tRmaZM7kEYJlKD1Ni8RcJf6cbGMcFvsWPINxzopTOyrTd9u7->  The company said the automated direct-deals business that Connect is enabling has grown on a percentage basis recently. The announcement follows recent news <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5cY9Ja9el9_WWjPMBufcvP6Nj_-YRKpUmhMmYSH2lHUEseZ7Zvg_-CMx0nUhrtQjNK_99uue_GCjWW4Ug9auke856GCzQCMxkeBJIyjaDbHVlQgA-MZv0CL7k-xNYtrc91uNQ4nLSYWxoEJA_TxFR9pyC1KmVXe0qbPBlTD4DkfxjcH8hactNXCmtL8n4oZIS6DSBvy6Tlt8pszs14nwPBnZqI7YkMnOMkAPTJK5n78Vw==>  from PubMatic about its mobile products and marketplace. The SSP is diving at mobile. AppNexus has positioned similarly <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5f1MstHt3EiE-DTXlDNtFcphCcMOrIkDtXDElhrc2K8sDPk6x02pSAAquukBnSed5553Tkw9Iw_3uuKu6s77w1shVfp9Mu0C8bvQe7Z6E7tblm84jYf2WwNa88uNsg9CXfPV02zOyCQVET7854sRnIF8P4smfmArxKP1yGdcciFeWlP16wVnmq5ba13OE4jNiw=> .

 

Bow To The King

 

Brian O'Kelley is heralded as the king of ad tech, at least by Forbes. In a profile of the successful co-founder and CEO of AppNexus, Alex Konrad paints the picture of a man who is difficult, but effective. "We are talking about leaving a real legacy here, not just on a small part of the industry, but on all the Internet. We are what pays for the Internet," O'Kelley said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5cTGKWRSLMdmBrj-ijq_MH2UPGmwgoOAVthMKApm3tVh9pLCBIqP-nUJUtN3ZSnk0M82O6phFeGlReu8ATJxizr8Qb3lOM3wBOAQQWbvRWhi_x07K-y9LLLAd7u25gBmW77meWBNEjBigwbKHXOtBB1i6xouxfJOS7FOzwpDthVdloSQQ4GKMajiqOX6w4cS7w3-cdYVLKoJZpu5YTvp_pl> .

 

Sponsor Apps

 

App search engine Quixey is adding sponsored results to its platform in an effort to begin monetizing. "This is our first foray into advertising," Tomer Kagan, Quixey's co-founder and CEO, told TechCrunch. "But we are experimenting with everything." The algorithm for sponsored results is similar to the one used for regular results, but it will also take into consideration things like app reviews and sentiment. The company has no plans to charge for its API. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5cbYuLNd1oNX3USp_P-jDo1qgXbamxhevE7P0qhTSbourkVQgNWJMKxb5Rsg1qz0QwKWBjDBfOu88__5O1N0mGjCHDITY-UdztS3qAasePczB7bCpHtD8XwVim2nmkdZ99calslVOK0Jr-GFq40NQEd5XK9Y8U1cqHLv2sXG6QQjCFCM2auYaGqYqFHFVSAZ5SAChXvYfZFOniPGDrdB_011SSK-Fw-HqwbZbusG6-uXrlyPkTeM-LuiWh42yImQnE=> .

 

New Programmatic Mobile Player

 

Gradient X, which says it's a real-time bidding mobile ad platform, is officially out of beta, according to a press release. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5evmAeFb7Ohn6ZX5uJcW8b7-NRi-Tphg5hjYEBwzHxk8OJW0oZ43dERamtaMGXlquKpLxbki9z5pYlbVAptd2FDQkjxhbLhTZGqnqF6NbYs4E6Bw5JmFo1qARcXo2MlB6HWtA-gWRT6EOS_zI_agZNaQU4AFEMBmC8=> . TheNextWeb is reporting that Gradient X has raised $3.75 million so far, and worked with brands such as Western Union, Jeep and Microsoft. According to the company, it is "the most advanced programmatic marketing platform for mobile available today." Doing Programmatic

 

ChoiceStream's Bill Guild offers some tips on iMediaConnection for programmatic buying, and flexibility is the name of the game when it comes to targeting. Targeting should be refined and, in cases where the audience is unknown, test pixels or polls should be used. Guild writes, "As with all aspects of technically driven advertising, targeting is something that works best in a real partnership. Trust what you know, trust your partners and work together." Kum-bay-yah. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5dHYYA1yinNXdynq5X3TGYmpD7e2lV1v1GLqfMem6ygx2AnEQ6X4X1CqkISnMYi5s7s-KmdpiCYfSn99w4NoDRBRPk9cH6pGQyro0__jlIp9obGOJF4STPUVcY8EudJ4apRhEWAF2CiwN3pIkeJmsPVIkI6XAM_ROPvpKMo710OXuwRHRteP1qP2tiIg7ct4e27SpWa1BGQMGDbGczu_0Cy7UNPhVBjxxQFf83LusVwOSID2bcBPpna0ekFMKJofBTCML_0PM_GFLkbcEjisl_mIIvxkSAk0h0=> .

 

FTC Gets Search

 

The FTC has updated its guidelines for ad disclosure in search results, according to ClickZ. Among the most notable differences are social searching, such as Facebook's Graph search, and audio results from Apple's Siri product. In all cases there must be a clear distinction that a search result was paid for. The FTC also pointed out that traditional search engines that have relied on shading to differentiate results must continue to do so and to make sure it's clearly visible on all monitors and screen sizes. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5cwYHVVnTPtlQE2-8cmgPeZD-LzK9YljSqLXI5iSLjgT9AEzxsBe7uY7hfDKq8S2hyd5IMmROwSr_cZUGnVL12ETkSVWKKsQ3H-__gqT1DlhUaQSGKtxdudagfcYJrAk8JXBMYC01ypHj_Pp1AM24EI4Wmzq1pIH5sPrViNO1z12E3UyMNf3mjbGfxvXLMOIXVzEt743Yxw7zr9NOhYwkTP> .

 

Banner Bad. Native Good?

 

Banner ads are bad, but native advertising isn't always much better, according to Traction CEO Adam Kleinberg. In a column for Ad Age, Kleinberg writes, "Native advertising has been heralded as the latest white knight of digital advertising, here to save us from ineffectual banners. But this brings up a new question: Who is holding native advertisers accountable for quality?" Among the major problems with native advertising are relevancy and disclosure, he says. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5dnv15E6ygbdt68Lx99Xf6W79IGAxw9M687DyBPYINEtbjvGEZ0e_oRR8iMrfy8xKGn-0I-f1IPp7LjmGpp4KqBVbHyySxgxbJYq3FLZPds0pcRvD2d_Pg_kkJmu02G34gBz2D1HUABigHIOs6ZIKziitWIOXluROdM456wNsKOMDNFMR4gNYO0-g-HCBBI5bE=> .

 

TV Style Targeting

 

Should video advertising be modeled after the traditional TV standard? Google thinks so, and it's launched a new tool called Affinity Segments, which allows brands to target ads on YouTube based on interests and demographics. According to a blog post, Mazda Canada tested the new tool and experienced "overwhelming success." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5doEnqbz-tNqcBeI-_TAXIwlukBPYYtO5Ol7giSLMK0ubGp8Ywl-7u5LBKrA_zzf2bPB6C0tOQg6POtIwiVGjz8e5ydajPW85V3A_hoPm-liBf8mbHAKaIIsyf0vaDoJcdsmUFJqH49oOB-sUMDM7Fd0Y3-hHeBsacsaKlb8QrmSCu7TfzCyHBP> .

 

Email Providers Retargeting

 

Like Responsys <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001jpsQ0nLuh5f7sMbVhoxjFLeltbT9LaZmT4ySa0KTjdmzItte7bJ7-L9ZFYLxDojM8hRY4MAjez2zGqueowsnQ3rWQiSnlh90hCTOHXV2mWpHtC64PQImOZtQfZSArpDgd92-DZbodFNbwNjzjpXZNIUfTldrg_QuZILaiPFcbn4=>  and others, email services provider StrongMail announced yesterday that it's adding display-advertising capabilities to its email services -- with the help of an unnamed partner, confirms a company spokesperson. The release claims, "StrongMail also makes it easy to insert email display retargeting into any cross-channel campaign, whether triggered, batch or a multistep lifecycle marketing program." eBay Refining Search

 

eBay continues to reinvent itself by rolling out a new search engine and refocusing its brand from just an auction site to a "global commerce platform." In an interview with Wired, eBay's Chief Technology Officer, Mark Carges, said, "It wasn't just that it needed a new coat of paint. We had lost our innovative approach to building software." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbMhlZHz_mOgzcfdPWMnMdd3FIED39aWtsDIHGb1QtAN__vCzgHhVRczU3q_fyOjdgcTY_c0XTyWoWd1Ng7gTUomVxaFUF7zP17Rhc7TupGo1zs9qLhWVC4eqr10hr9XQajd61HE4yw-doaqoWlWFenfYLgY_IHYBHP7Gp_2yLUPkw==> . Though unmentioned, "retargeting," which leverages more accurate search data, could aid eBay's advertising business strategy.

 

Programmatic Jobs

 

In an effort to bolster its global programmatic advertising options, AOL announced 40 new job openings in Dublin. "Nowadays, agencies and advertisers want to move to the real-time realm, where they are able to, from their perspective, get the best possible value at any given instant for their ad spend, and from a publisher perspective get the best possible revenue for their impressions. So when you move to real-time you have to move to a programmatic type of buying and selling because it's too quick for human intervention for the most part," said Aengus McClean, head of AOL Global Operations. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbOjDnqaIlTIAmuvY67YVrhhGzc1cxsd9-Qfw9iDrNBMPlyg6aSjOC1RmzCHYO-wgJV419mdmmmT-4Pw5HJ4UU7vO4141rrVWSVrOzq5LObWUqxaOF0JuhvmfB575RB2sYYS94-SYYkkt53YMBGBeRiqq7t_bFMKikY=> . The Silicon Republic, which covered the story, also compiled a list of memes related to software engineering jobs. See those here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbNiW6ePjJoQOqa8gbtPQj_2bAPyBzYQcztBuF5bLBLeAtS4bX_LELzyg0PkFok72cXawL9hkZkj-EYxu1hAWEPCoXG59eygMQ4pcX7vxVJ54xj5y9qma8H5yvBarQ7Uz_MOXioX7tHfL_XvTYfUdA_oFXR9PIskVUpCexaqSN6_1w==> .

 

Inadco Is Back

 

As part of its announcement regarding an $11 million funding round, Inadco says it is adding search and social to its display-ad, lead-generation product line. CEO James Walker says the funds will be used for R&D and to build products. The company appears to be capitalizing on the native ad craze, too. Its boilerplate explains that the company provides "a platform for marketers to create native ad units called Form Ads that enable two-way communication between consumers and marketers, allowing for real-time data capture." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbP2KNp_6Q0qJH0MW7KN_Y_jfvd-Cd4BOMTbQYf4yGSKs13aH3nD35VLRLDArIbmeI8AqZqxdZ6M9vWhCZ4MFmi8GeRVVgG3XJaE3vMrQWPTy3-DF0Yje3a0iS0-_essRkvlULkUqUgGc1RhJ3UJgcHb0Piju6gI41_Zq0jbLNkIp6oYkjScwRKs5XYjuIX7M_N2G5yDTsSpa1CVpX3hFVhG> . And, read this Inadco 2011 interview with AdExchanger <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbODfz0a0ei8o6yySjd1huh7Kp0iWWaT_FYySzfjKKlv_5j2_PUiLOmiOc7gDTDvQWzY9ucJ3Vqy1h_2ypajAfQH-UxhNr6eQr_HjCP9To0UcQLeNq7cXKPu-hH3YuUvcUgRgJWoru2ivw==>  which explains some of the basics of their leads biz.

 

Ad-droid

 

According to the developers of the Lookout app for Android, 6.5% of free apps (out of a sample of 200,000 apps) meet their definition of adware. "The small minority of ad networks that behave badly is making a lack of trust for the entire industry," Lookout's Jeremy Linden told the MIT Technology Review. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbOawLGZ4sq9lFjRtm1KHdqzE6g1vsZ_XxzLU3_jjXP1s_GAW1ZbaLp6CXUI8Whaa-VI8Muya5UdIzstQjlbi-AiI-8DI2gl-v_Ias1Fdox5t4ZGNp4q9c8BYB98cz-M7G5N2-4AdHI8VYp2t3uT6_uF__pr7eivp5rMh7nhpz2sXNWFQU4B9YkzhEK2W5XVroj__FOeNCl2WWgL90dycbDm> .

 

Existential Ad Tech

 

In an article from The Drift, Doug Weaver draws a parallel between a line on Mad Men and real life. The quote: "If you don't like what they are saying about you, change the conversation." Weaver goes on to say that if people aren't talking about your company, you have to give them a reason to do so. He writes, "Do anything but 'introduce yourself.' First, they will care that you've brought an agenda that's about them; then they'll get emotionally connected with the problem or issue you're prepared to take on; then - and only then - will they want to know your bio, credentials and track record." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbNBdjc6jN7-AqjHC412PRBGhttE6lUYORTCR811UkuhxZIfH0YYd97lsibhBhE6oF9QgnzmMvyMIUF_9_uhgX_CXphbueGTxz1Wopc59sWd5iqZNEzm7Uaqrxyk4bTIbe_yj9Wqq7ikRA==> .

Mayer's First Meeting

 

Marissa Mayer held her first stockholder meeting since taking over as Yahoo CEO last year, and according to Silicon Beat it went well, aside from a couple of interesting moments. The first came when a group of Walmart employees tried to distract from the topic at hand, which was Yahoo. The second was an older shareholder who was distracted by his attraction to Mayer. Yahoo has had five CEOs in five years. One shareholder said this meeting was more fun than the previous two. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbMJH9f6n12KtMouXeM8dL85IBLL8qHMkZgNvwqX-_mSO-FfuLlA343Lm9r8CHr5z3rLttEyeyN0xpw0frp5absY_E7sy4QBZlDaP1ELBj2JFu7EcdQUDynnqhEnkJGOBKN9AmHGhZ-JqdKmtpkny4LpF-hwV4l1wFimEALOzmjsFoCpn68kWuBvxNZvicsItc7ATvfMNYAlBw==> .

 

Search And Display

 

On Search Engine Land, Magnetic VP of Tech Ops Lionel White wonders aloud about the future of Facebook search and display -- a topic near and dear to Magnetic's heart. He concludes, "We don't know how long cheap prices will hold out, how much display inventory will be available on Facebook's exchange and how quickly Graph Search will be adopted by its massive user base. Only time will tell just how much value Facebook will bring to the search and display markets." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NVwSZfG_HbPoUHjZqOxVjxHDn4CWUIygQ4kEaezgD0bm7OYjlC1TM-m0E7rOA4VkAL80u07awbZesZ2f8WqgKoYwy1voKw4HpxvcXPPzdIyxaDgTW3zlvmt512QVZttx_D-D5-h_WhYpiL_Beu_tpv5Tm-F1O1iT1I8kiwRBErn26oKwPGi-SVOKbF4GS9ac> 

 

Recommending Intent

 

Internet Retailer says Nordstrom has taken an equity stake in gift-recommendation site Wantful.com. A Nordstrom spokesperson tells IR, "The fastest-growing part of our business is e-commerce. You have to find better ways to personalize the [online] experience." War Of The Cookies

 

If browser company Mozilla accomplishes nothing else with its intention to block third-party cookies by default, it at least got people talking. This time it's IAB's Randall Rothenberg who criticizes Mozilla for its efforts, saying, "It is not a clearinghouse for cookies -- It is a kangaroo cookie court, an arbitrary group determining who can do business with whom. It replaces the principle of consumer choice with an arrogant 'Mozilla knows best' system." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGodjOGuIm7etzb5nYvFZOo7900wjATQaq7GyDu3_SGcRyi_m98FHCK-8fZzdaToSlonHDyPr_dNS2_pdlSikQ9k0eIzr0UzUZkjUTSSJqQknl8YPuUJz8ZsFEbldaVqgo2UqM7kE44OBymYcdf2fIYoa_VHUXhrN3NrPaU0An_QaxS7v7s506J1> .

 

Ad Spend Down

 

Ad spending declined the first quarter of this year compared to last year, Ad Age's Michael Sebastian is reporting. Decreases are attributed to year-over-year comparisons where the Olympics and the presidential election spawned unusual increases in ad spend. Also: "Data from the early second quarter are mixed, suggesting marketers are still being cautious and conservative with ad budgets," said Kantar Media's Jon Swallen. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGrpQGQ0IKTLxcIt1VYlz7c-xNu1GhDKjPSkSEO9BWCWldPYL7pcSjp1t_rVdzY88czSG4ROx2bc6RvnQBlNQ4UuLxWA3HwnEjmP-7Pb_jq_7cAyd2ajfVTpG0V_CKKx6zkyVRDEo3QvRh2F4e3CsiiGRV24eUzkJCm6vyYnuIlbDA==> .

 

Global Malware



GigaOm's Jeff Roberts reviews Google's latest Transparency Report, which sheds light on malware infecting the World Wide Web, among other nefarious data points. "The highest rate of malware ... doesn't belong to obvious suspects like Russia or Ukraine (8% each), but instead India (15%) and many Latin American countries like Mexico (12%) and Chile (11%)." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGr9sBlxsNSR1Iv-SKoRRP24LvyAcTBdzHtKxCPqkcCinUpEkAWIU_qohRef3-_ctOlnz9k8HOHTGerQy_W2R4lxnIG1Nz7ny-58fiG6vuwY1PD4CPIsOkr-rptJZfWAn98NYjsrcha5zwr4Nb0upjn9YV8UDlSluyhrFG80aR5icKgncY9_fBa-MfnMoVf56LHalwWtCbAmKTyslbD6di0HB1mOC4lTIktFb6VMbRi7vQ==> . And see the Transparency Report <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGqgF10ptwLsmOICHc2mEpsuniC2u9HRJVkkjGZcNuqL0pPm-a4WgQ-5ncvAPYPhAmMCdwPLrg6XsC-hrwIweySBbckQQ5N7dyrD3ixfdjD_5S4EPWZML106Va5lOjuY4TfTyHnF7cXecWugTQWlDKlIPHC9DLD06iBGsBNXH2sQ5aFD0kDMvJu1d4ciEaQzRWrT_KXKNk1JVnXWDzDfN2vmN5iiy9eXUdrsinQnSQ9DbQ3HRM1pd4j-EM0PjfiftjlmnICg878FETdW4WyE5-ijOvNY73KWhaQ=> .

 

The Debt Trend

 

Following other startups' moves into the world of borrowing (Triggit <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGqBSekiajlBhVClnmQruRnrydrwgOU6WkWMM1r0EZr6vNdV6CV39lzEw2s-D7SqAriQ_tVTmRgK6Grgo-NWQ1PRQdKurLoeyW1I1Md8_54wW1hRDZUTzlFURji2nClIcG56ovqx893NRrGuFNxYWbO83lO-Ja0t8q8mG5vB5dkWFZe4HKHmmIcKgyjKasi_4BtOgriw3buoHg==> , Lotame <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGqk8wk8Tc5L5P48QyH1XH6q0lO-9joxeQgEW3mCucu4HxO-d76jxxxatO50JqHQm2q4e3ey87pKmwbocN9KpzkJxAq8A3uJq_BNj17dqC00jNX0FA76G6LvG2z1n6x44sRv--Ryj9QkcHF1qbTpVu-pQB4MW2mzOCyyb1q2LcYD3aCGQDoEJh80OUL5Ep3WDoE=> , and [x <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGqVryom2FTNUrPomlhohrqiW4hztvfS6YC7dii3oYJeTGhgOed4-8Rmchxn4VqR8kh6oR84gpyF_PPae8kp_wyQTxQYFS7JwsnFX7NCUTvAaDqxH_kVqyOFZNwAwHAjxifoOxaMKTzza8D1ike_zdfp> +1], to name a few), and rather than risking further dilution, b2b data manager and ad platform Bizo announced $12.5 million in financing yesterday. It previously received nearly $16 million in capital from investors, says Crunchbase. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGrbItXGVrl_lJfcme4dMMX_yQY-Yw3RlB9lcokgZ3Tuj_SXVvM-EbBibNnziQyNwBvhXsW6-5C3ntCrLmLz_LUDiEQ1qsCN_TsEbsJIUic6qDZCQ_gX3F1x5hIR3j0j_mkwmfMnPslw62amEviWmcnT2ov8o4YF6GDkT8sq03EzdC3D-TMlb9M1HQqnfCGYd_P4-HkdUFbtfQ==> . The company, which was spun out of Zoominfo in 2008 <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGr6OlNK_G6o1EC6JU_51yvYxFfZcrZ2Do1Y3o4kUrqzxnsCY-Y0RhYNtqlGbcedVKbfb1-bwvV9zC0hfEKxOvAkrGWAUJ0buS1TOC6CB944GVpB0O7FLAsDzmWNrNgqZfYRNuzaZLNdXEscHPoOx-BWHx0v_5lXQf91J8oRUN7WB0yp97V0WjoMX9s2SkODRJz0JUd7FekueWLQbihaqVRWfwOTV3xapSUrRqS08rn2Tw==> , said media and data deals running through its platform are producing a (presumably "gross" rather than "net") annual run rate of $40 million. Also, read AdExchanger's May interview with Bizo CEO Russ Glass <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGpj4I3MGHim6Hizuxrx9426VdFvfGJsRQin8O8CJjVu6_taQZHnfq2Eo-UisKTmB4Bs5khkbvg_OEU7nd7sMtGTVaPC82k6sSrNJKSIJIYqgW3Jl78DCWP6ndA8aGJCVUQ1HyCjsPzhc0Gwzknf-BYtrjKpg9DFRLs8-drKD_VmHQ9tAxbccfRU> .

 

FBX Road Trip

 

Facebook's Exchange is adding travel data courtesy of Adara (among others), which aggregates booking data directly from airlines and hotels. From the release: "A hotel chain or rental car company can serve ads about their Hawaii properties or rental car rates to people on Facebook who searched airfares to Honolulu. Or, a mobile communications provider could advertise international service packages to travelers on Facebook who booked flights overseas." More. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGr77cRa7w8fjKyb5psuX3jYIEN1q5mglTAULBibQQPX1y3hjhb9AmLSdcH8_yPp_DlUKxN7BeTbLvfRkm8i_TK7JEenSs2iIGeTxqmq5w88HEewr1cuHABmYfkrPm41M4rkhezsYLMe2CQ9T89RQxow1atfI6bYELKpus28bMQJJGzMY5OZD_-E6htbIjNwGhA=>  Adara at one time sought to pivot away from the travel vertical (AdExchanger story <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGpnZCprBcXPlSiZzN2k4KnVgETdp89Ry0ZixSFqe8tSh3VG9ldprPgfUiQOO-fJmKDvq7gVehFf_w6exEyo4zwDcTgn_HeRd1vZqG8BWDl-40IaFd8HU0Bd1SLip6WNvMEiFoaOuFF-NH5NjQ4q990Pa4h8zrEfoefIhb0juEfBp4uRbbQTC072cI2ZzBWQF1dDMG6r1LKl1A_reNhB4te02fwkkn7icU402OPFOMrRI0iFvLSfUBcjT6pFesu_xJ4EYR0nArW1Rw==> ), but has retrenched.

Programmatic Tweeting

 

Twitter added five new partners to the ads API it opened in February: Kenshoo Social, Optimal, SocialCode, SocialFlow, Unified and Voxsup. According to a Twitter blog post, the company will add new partners on a rolling basis. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGootd1skIMkEPP53kGhc_9YuwLtwNMow3q-A_N-BePwoKfUn0GV_3I1WvTd7AB_xiXzZum773pT6_9ggjvCQbeTR3YUfqQpa5-VCDfseZ9lnoR_qpw88PNwtBw7vS99techx421XMEdsMdDi0XWtiPAhT8qozrWQOqAqfIawxrgGDELZY9b8bj-r7C_hMyn9DUhZgcGXYuQjA==> . All Things Programmatic

 

Still in doubt about programmatic? Mondelez's Bonin Bough predicts a future when programmatic buying dominates all channels, according to The Drum, which covered his participation at the Cannes festival last week. "TV is probably going to be traded on digital exchanges sooner and more rapidly than digital itself was - everything will be programmatic buying," Bough said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001bRbcBAK9PGqEQf6WbQGRfuiACdWmVDT2DTlnRG6j577TswOrXm0OOpy5f0YGbhk9UAuO0nX7hzQFz6vaz5kynhjkhA9kpGLLxx7rF4I04SA-KCgp8tZ_kZ435VzuWLHULPXPVCObwO0IC2dj-VeAaMh0aqgSL1DbvIMpD7ONAS1kQ5Onlic88nFofoAw-IG5wRd6IF5wTplWAWAeJgrAXXBOFKx6VW41HbIBMZaPALc=> .

Shaving Performance

 

Convertro is helping Dollar Shave Club attribute performance offline -- on TV -- says a new article from Ad Age's Kate Kaye. She explains that Convertro "measures direct navigation to advertiser websites, or searches by brand, comparing the number of those actions to the number of people who visited the advertiser's site before the spot ran. The spot information comes from post-log data -- the information that shows where and when TV ads actually ran, rather than what was ordered. Pre- and post-log data can differ quite a bit." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnpyXemXN5ry6EQsi4ET_KA1EjGYa4Osyf0__NIi4-wFtypRyVBa67FvXfTK2ZpZCWaESMYQkb_1Ek16xmPx9iVQp9y6beZds2_TfHFqf7EkuPHbwY6zJBW18niua3pUxlH0MPKAeXOdzTVoFzHKjfdKof1LWw1ARnlR2fxxv1sMUFnHy2mTxKELtJD4ftC00dWRPd4EpDxkw53UnZvO_h8KiEWtQK3u7iI=> 

 

RTB To Go

 

There's a new mobile RTB player in town, RTB.com (was Manage.com <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnqCNhf7wC1yqWbIFHF7n6vgfzCYwHI-NY4ls-QrwAQ9mYE92KD_Ui5ScmbvS4JzpEIaGb1UHJkpfnrLnl7786mwuvi7JX2-fncY-j4a0utivhJoSBj1aTv3> ), according to MediaPost. The company was founded by Fred Hsu, also a co-founder of Oversee. "The platform monitors the RTB stream, billions daily, and when we see a user on a specific device, knowing their location, we'll determine the user's worth, maybe a fraction of a penny, before making a bid," Hsu said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9Dnqq-i5s-t_SvDbMMi6wrlJP43zRozd4AYC6_1TBCuzyXiMLPxJejSp3bOqBnICaUoWY9Mh6KIhLmu4dyq5mu4CMBtGHmPrKZhyKU0hem21hFAeADRU3hUbquo-1CPnQurZAfeHHcwnkNUlYXK3LF6m_cOK_E823HZ3XSDMiwhwUysrXXCMzxJmOS7sCH97XZ4mSApUlC91vgzsyiO6xpJpHrQ3-ASttGGKCI6Kn2S4FLL9bCfM_c3_pCBV5JlFkD1NqNm39rL5fJvVQUzzoeNt2> . Everybody is catchin' the wave.

 

Mobile Puzzles

 

Solve Media, known for its puzzle-like CAPTCHA system, has launched a mobile platform for advertisers to get users interacting with ads. According to a blog post on their site, Unilever and Songza are already using the TYPE-IN platform. "Solve Media's Mobile TYPE-IN™ ads drive stronger economic results for us while maximizing the time that our users can enjoy the soundtrack of their lives interruption-free," says Elias Roman, CEO of Songza. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnrsfFxBYInXw70bXCsMZWegIaRLCuqSZWtlFzmQb3Jgz2N9IXy18-a2t1j8JlGOXOn7kuDQiSRQc4kStsEjSBiWFTJ6tvtaPaixnT5QHpogIahr6nNkV5HYRgTXJXQs9HnyRXpQCNmEoSUIU5BD2FaHdDZsotHDPFw4czfB0yPPDMwOYbcz4W5Z4rCBeVnKzeUnZKCV23Nz35dVNQTi6sXx> .

 

Local Twitter

 

Data analytics startup Topsy is getting to the local level through location data on Twitter, helping advertisers reach audiences at the right place and the right time. As AllThingsD's Mike Isaac points out, there are a host of issues to be ironed out such as the need for repeat references and accuracy only at the country level. "Instead of just being there when the lights go out at the Super Bowl, we're trying to offer real-time engagement at a local level at any time," said Jamie de Guerre, SVP of Product and Marketing. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnpDbWo4ZtpAZRN1QOWvBDIF3CfUMM-go2MEXTk_xKY9dZJ-pnz9pl7asja907ELvruhY27XqjIjE0Je-eekUK9w-WVFsqBngVBHNdHWxTcAbvxsPgvph8BPkhfj7ICv6mri6sP2uPIwIbTZ5dpkgJnHsNHWUXk0G0cMFybvoIL6CIHIgIHfIPRYHFYNDT57ri4=> .

 

Consumerizing

 

B2B marketing is evolving to a more consumer-like approach with Buzzfeed running a GE-sponsored content campaign called Flight Mode, according to Digiday. "The people who influence and make large B2B purchases are the same people who enjoy consuming and sharing news and social emotional content on BuzzFeed," said Jon Steinberg, President and COO of Buzzfeed. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnqjQnImtCARiZj2EpImd6vwC0Ahg-58W7BWnai9hlzQgthcAvZBb0Hhq1hzSuL1eNznnVv06BWTs9jmAKZdWLUj0FpI73MD-1y4UmN22oDhzkvZK7ApZMAtc3TpCKaSzjEtyotDNpNOOZBo9Q3TprWV1gElVKBX4c5w0uZZE_2cUA==> .

The Start of Something New

 

In a sign of the times, Samsung is dumping its desktop computer business to focus on its mobile computing products, the Korea Times is reporting. "The connected world is going to expand. This is the industry's new trend. Simply put, desktop PCs are no longer a cash-generator. Samsung is getting smarter," said Kim Il-tae, a senior fund manager at Taurus Investment. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnrTdF9NnOCUqyiXjT5SmGi0rUAGBfdoO-9i5YdhM_2dxo4Y9K1-_1bqNLG6pvEAby0v_C7TcJ6eDH92UyNLVy2QyPVgqUsCOGF7Q5Irq7OPECpQwwFbmFdSNOMYJIbCqI8pxrU6dBEM_X29GpnD_A8J9A9ZT1tmAvMHqbm1FWidf8PzoydYfd4Y> . A Gartner report echoes that sentiment, citing a decrease of 10.6% in desktop computer shipments along with tablet shipment increases of 69.7%. Read its report <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9DnqDCFr4o1_xNzKgAJTBXDFKUw5cnx_im3zK63aC0WUfcjfGCg9AZkpJTo3qC_4ivZx6tWwXnzz2SrfhNPMjbFdogA2Ozw-I2kZ9bRIwcsIJZPdQ3oN05mUgfQv734tqizYJFzOYfO20-A==> .

 

The Republic Of Data

 

We now know the government collects data on citizens through the technology it uses, but in Andorra one man wants to take data collection and turn it into a lucrative ad business, according to Fast Co Labs. "The goal is to develop a platform that is sourced with data from the telecom, energy provider, installed sensor infrastructures, the bus company, tourist buying habits, store directories, store inventories, restaurants, etc. and to make it available to researchers, entrepreneurs, and companies as a tool for understanding and experimenting with new technologies and ideas," said Travis Rich, director of technology of the Smart Country program. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ZmwAu7T9Dnpeym9O1DUsZxBDPA_A7YQeWDpykFuL4CSUg9uykbOZCweoJIkjBjz8RysjePA15AAu3it7ZLLoF7GzSe_jpBXdnd_xBzpAwT9Ge5jG4C8G_u-hzXS3aJNXrVVmmD-G5hB-WeuO9X0uVMTef4sCX-CGoHu3nYbuh63lMxicDYSofTGZ5Fztnw_WRvx2xiVyZie78dwu1F1NEA==> .

Unparting The Clouds

 

Oracle and Salesforce may be transitioning into a new phase of co-opetition - or maybe you prefer "frienemies"? The New York Times breaks the news, "Next week, according to people familiar with the agreement who were not authorized to speak on the record, Oracle and Salesforce will announce that their products will be able to easily share data." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcszpwEWz290LMl84Hdi8QGMrDiN83rnsII6cMEP7R1owBNvj2qwJp-Yqala8B7-jIE7qLrMZZbE4LYtP_2fsbTIMJygDvZVGc6ciHk2WUgMfq_xeiNF-LbEcCG0lJN2gXiJmQWj_JvcrYWYAFlnsX1QXKBWpewOpFFadudldBPS77lJBOr2kmZEoZAbC75SkQEj27Ag9Ttv9W3jt_IWCBI0> . Apparently, Oracle and Microsoft will be unveiling a new partnership today, too, says the NYT. You gotta partner to thrive (and survive)?

 

Live Audience Buying

 

Ticketmaster's Live Nation says it wants to turn its "live" events business into a media company, which means making the most of the consolidation of 14 databases with 400 million customers.  That's a lotta potential online-offline addressability.  Live Nation CEO Michael Rapino explains to The Financial Times, "We know you're going to be at the venue, we're talking to you along the way. We have your email address, your mobile phone...and then I can put a banner or a sample on the seat you're about to sit down on." Sit here (subscription). <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcszGEEA40sNa8g4Ea9oiF-ziRPaBTxpBL5o2pvnOTisA9KdcoygvFGp6N7YUj4NHU2FAwXzOjcwmUbjX1SvzqH8dpTr2HBkhbuH9-WhqlgAM27ovAgnwmpw5CFt8Gbsa3QwRLlezCV5DB0vD-pCKZnAWY92qNz3P0ND3k_M7kDgw-a-TEe5SgD9WCowe5m8Mn6D6XfQJ_AfUA==>  


Demo Ads

 

Mobile advertising isn't limited to banners and videos, which Agawi hopes to prove with its AppGlimpse platform that allows game developers to advertise via demos on Android and iOS. Although the ads will be cross-platform, as of right now only Android games will be advertised, according to TechCrunch's Anthony Ha. "In the long-term there is a strategy for even using iOS versions of a game to create ads. It's a significant engineering effort, but we'll get there," Co-founder Rohan Relan said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCctl2cS84Bq5ru8cveO45pGS-9KLmDwl94vQPPZKVvrDgUzERfjGL8hw39zstABmpsp47UP41IOAlqFn7eC7YgC_mRgFpox0TbxeO-dxyVNqz5-jgwdvfhu7uvmWai4nRvs71j0VwLDswCtHKKt8oj5xWfaevtTrH5VpxDRTsu35AQ==> .

 

Mobile Video Ads

 

Millennial Media was busy late last week with product announcements. No word on the exchange they mentioned <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcvOMKokgydP63bfMKeynorykH-pxHrVyR0RA6cYAS8NPuHPj043ync-WO9wi51nUQB8MBLYa-BSDT1mSVrHryDzWEB3zFpECOtI3Kg4UUwtfRMG_vP5FUE--9l5YU4DqYDyXk-iRcxCTtpCf0Ljn7NFOOvsrkP5r1o1XIqarVkyRg==>  in their earnings conference call in May, but there will be nine new video products offered to advertisers that allow for smartphone and tablet optimization along with a bevy of dynamic creative options. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcuT0eFF_tta3UywGuftperNmGx_cZkkKAJGlc9CETKJB00o8vGClHMO9m-AlXjfxDcsL6eG0o7OVfsc8LUezf5Hr6nHh7cHzV-VacLfbKGJ6-Zwa72ZxtbSbbHboq6-phkI1xsZZPSBXLx1HHeFJvaPT7XWqtgoD9V5uAAOGyV4avqnvLfUCUdHxaB9jOYuXn2IzBccPK5LJ8pT6yMy6Xdu--kecfbWQ8R4CoXeJX-1_99psWofIRmedLWR93UEi60=> .

 

Geo-Tweeting

 

Twitter continues to beef up its ad product, this time adding a geo-targeting feature for retailers that would send users a tweet when they are close to the store. According to Ad Age, there is no official word on when the feature will be released, although its likely to arrive by end of year. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcu8ky-IqLtnxtJ18w1y4zZsMTuiueaOy0QBdh1FoxBeVRFB7EDcfh2PFVvwmIYHcJYIyS5xUG3Tp9u8Banhd-HcbxL6rNKOx1y7pvldGrEWuAojXTzVc9NTVREIMRGKjSbJNfvAMZyEMbfo6-DYNUP3hBPzytn2hO0WEvENSFToT8W_3rnil3XbgcN8aPeqC8Bc1DWRnGliWQ==> . Assuming the product comes to fruition, it will be interesting to see how Twitter creates rules for advertisers, and controls for consumers. Separately, Twitter's knowledge on real-time geo-location and the permission it gets with the use of its app, could provide targeting data that informs digital ad buying environments outside of Twitter.

Global RTB

 

The use of real-time bidding (RTB) is fairly widespread globally, but there are still a few regions playing catch up. According to Sociomantic CEO Jason Kelly in MediaPost, the U.K. is on par with the U.S. in terms of data-driven advertising, but advertisers in Russia are just learning what RTB means. He offers, "Within the Russian market, RTB is still frequently confused with retargeting. Most often, RTB is perceived as a way to buy cheap remnant impressions. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcsDQ7eg5LHcwcglWOwJsbb2nvLJG-DpML100LfLOm0dgQQRWRvzA3AoLzqo52eVlvRzCkTIuhcuUNuY639VDBTxTV0QpeVIZxQTLEuMQEzFVRWENv7lwQ2RsX3Ap_oytQvKhulru_Dfxdq4CdpL-MeQwGceEvAwYLKrXkC9oNAX64Bd2vDJt7DlbaO3Y-EZjUZiCNX_VBGYVWb6l7zmK61cWCKn8E2LD6o=> .

 

Cross-Network

 

Calling itself "a self-serve cross-network ad campaign creation, deployment and management platform," AdStage added new funds (total raise $1.5 million+) and new hires including two former Googlers said the company. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001J4wMMCHUCcunhtqTh2q1nD42AzM0m7JCQma9schLH0_VgbsZQj4-GGV0yfaa7oLpOsewPkw0T7iFRyhn-d4i-i045yl1Y6KElyZh_SoRPzTOcJb8jWgNn7id_Sn2VehwFksa7hyM8xCNNFDmqAgB4W4X4PLE5dYHiSipKHkHXP5yjiKDmnSLNTb8q1uh3bGpoe7AosNE8bstKfJncYps6Afdeg_PL2hj9qE-3SVmvP8pGv6Xc8S9yZbyF1fQErTGxwUySGFlQB4Rb2qpeq6igdqRh7snGfvGRhbcD8HW7AYf1_D2pqDWSw==> . The company says it brings together different flavors of ad buying - such as Google, Bing, Facebook and LinkedIn - into one user interface and then optimizes accordingly. AdStage says it just bought Semply, too, which manages Adwords campaigns on the iPad.

Paywall Momentum

 

Shifting attitudes toward digital news are finally making online publishing a more lucrative business. So says Robert Picard, research director at the Reuters Institute for the Study of Journalism, who tells the Guardian that people seem to be more willing to pay for online news -- and that there's a proliferation of digital news consumption. Citing his research, he says, "A number of large publishers known for their traditional news brands are now generating 15% to 25% of their total revenue from digital media with audiences as much as 10 times larger than their print editions because the digital platforms attract new users." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d_XlnZUSppvrDnjvCrubosN9TgLshgoKntSGqZe4AcejhQ_W8bHOb0EzBPmfq7y836vzNeAJf9oYf5TEDzEmHf3AJ8mZViwRGgpByNoomV0YAawAzwRP5ArbZUMvDT7r0MAvk_NGLCNyjvJNKh55roPXWXqutCvroW-NK2QxbAsrtG6WuxW8ObQI-gV8-IsHtA=> , or download his research (PDF) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d_66pbWUSGHP1we4HjmCMWg0BOXO1HEQ_XeHRVzAVvIi_jteKa1dtwh7bW2vQz8FzJ8JnyIO1Z2fpS2xz0Ueb6ZNzWhykL1MOOyCZZXT6CfbCebswSWfaZG9XoQIci6NfXmUXgRHHvQ-BL-pR3rYun18UVImaIgjuc9XKie9TfxHfxKxdJxFKI36aUCZqH8ebkBDlGlSGMeaA7AFIYd-Ex6WuoqOc49R0A9lP25twKHpV_CO4RhpVg3> .

 

Instavideo

 

The rumors are true. Instagram now has video. Users can take up to 15 seconds of video and apply 13 filters to their content, similar to the way photos are handled. The product also has a feature called Cinema that will help stabilize shaky video, putting Facebook squarely in competition with Twitter's Vine product. Read the blog post here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d_Nfg46FqxGadVMY8-eCw2sdSCDe5RQy_kvH39BwyXHoFfg6YncQHl3sLPHON7-h64_qIvRAann-ccn18UXc1lVMipK76p24d_3H3LJMhlFpaKyMj1nq9HvVmYHs0UzHt5Pk6KDkgchy4144KQoRikKXrkmt6RhB2I=> , and watch the announcement here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d-aqf68SaRcic-OzY6-99bqBiplYWh1E3mEoI3V6hx_BdpVY_iL5Hsx0p8eIaAOkx0QHP5sd73pAgdIYIm8fGv5gf1zgt5zBrSzbO8WvXEPupeMyBPBLQMIwp5T6PebpikJuGBwzq_RGgTXKKFl9IryyFSGshs1AHI=> . Are addressable video ads on Facebook next? Survey says ... yes. But how do you pre-roll a 15-second video clip? Post roll. Write it down!

 

AdBrite Gutted

 

The AdBrite saga continues. First, the company brought on former Right Media executive Hardeep Bindra <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d_ePmNp2EUvd7wbQX0bljDq8a-Pdny5zb0p8ftKT24d1pag6ARuyCYOXtZYgjoF97IU-WpurBe-FUEk1aQ7d0t4FL33OOzlnjy8w_Rf5pLbn7JC2-oPnwI5uv5idG1mA0rkHBgRLbZYpqSVQC8DNnmxaE188K8fYgotgFlS4sTKD6Auf1iWGFDYmJY2LsRCSTcB6Y3LAkNd8zkaYU7hjXg2OOyvzWp7qpuP3auFT8_dwg==> . A month later it dropped its exchange <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d9rhQ9GNXHlSg3vKqvPy4mdp9fqpAGfjDr0a0_r3znPtOgRJLwPwD8LfJmFuZ--AWC7J61tgNUDCkMP7WYKF4zofXH-PDfR67o_xJcZx_vgBDoV2esxlW4Ztn_lGA7eB54daqrWCs6vCGLSUzDb3oy0HSxenq8ch62W9aajFhH2CREqnSthDElZ4tywKl-HRd16UL7pfA4GTG_gvZTQuw5gyVQ0yJAqI66fFQSywRDipg==>  -- and then it closed. Now, SiteScout announces it has acquired the IP assets from the former ad network. The AdBrite URL now redirects to SiteScout, and there is a Q&A up in a blog post here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d-2NBhGK6jsYSGO0XnKf2vwtQfkHK1iY4X0Ef3DmL2ulb_UY7f_AbouxJiS7s6HAkrIqhLa-yU0JqN0tj7PCMVMylStd4JtLqOw65xvnxAMtiqlVwC5KhyJUDJjW27983z6B9LcEjWnMAra_tdW2mV0EzOmsnTritD0tfM1kXbU4B2EQOF2euvC>  that discusses some of the changes. Read the press release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d9XeOteSW8tX_jmeZRVO13Zf2No7V5O1Nz7am-HZ2CvZThpHHkRDBq_lUluZeGDJf0jH99ZFDKW_EagIs-PFSjN_LL_wEshkwC9E2yfmy_7ya6T6rVEWthw51ZVGCZ5ZIt1DCNZ2P9FuQ9gSVhydmaI8m74_UI6sG7Tfd2u1luqhI70e6wdf7Tvq3M2QdABKkg=> .

 

QR Codes To CRM

 

QR codes live! So says Internet pundit Doc Searls in the Harvard Business Review. Searls also talks about Vendor Relationship Management, or VRM, which allows customers to manage relationships with multiple companies -- basically CRM in reverse. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d-gDsSFQf3nBXk-vlsOHpTjxBxlGDnNUOItKaEGYba--7z1mxOlcmtDgV7a3_a_oJCF1dALCXZ-YDikt8YM6_cw9UUUi0P9k24Cj4n4g__p5lyKUZMdBbwJDB0GSVCembd_AZmXoTtGNv2DNKupo12X17CYubaK9SrlMzjc4qLl-g==> .

 

Data Woes

 

Google continues to navigate stormy seas in the European Union over privacy issues -- this time in France, where the company is being given three months to amend its data policies or face fines. According to Bloomberg, five other countries will be following that lead in July with similar ultimatums for the tech company. The fines could get into the millions of Euros depending on which regulators and countries impose them. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d_wYgJNxVY4N4qn7zqzmgDm540pB4un1K2b3Y4HmN-QUbGcjbCaQy5Hj7P-vgINnAXIeNn8LM6s1v93bjgexIgeHWraUysHuUtAWvj5pOhGGOe94dsflqCqnpe7ZVwGzo9Aujoprh-or8YJ_t8pRRrVWDU8g8HUKxf0xVgNAxoMZhonbHixE-z6CojxXEqT2H1FBBsQFZE3fh-z1Bz9j8bZIfpbK8CgLt8eg7x8VLm-yQ==> .

Trading Traffic

 

Chartboost allows game developers to promote each other's apps, and a new group system will allow multiple developers to partner up and trade traffic, according to TechCrunch. "For most developers, it's never enough of a priority for them to build a platform internally unless they have so many hits in a row that they have money to invest in it. But we're democratizing access to the network technology," said Maria Alegre, Chartboost's CEO. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d9PVsQxrb3Su-SxudBe621HLqtwx0mNk0OZc4j4Us9JT-raayFMSA4gUuQlUowXaSHwA65EHuWQuue3AG1YpC4_UrH5hASB6FNEqwmaIZ5Iy-Tn-OmIxts8OdZm0G5mXeZNjYpc-PD477ngnrAeYUcErB0tEepBRu0=> .

 

Online Privacy Attitudes

 

Sir Martin Sorrell believes people's feelings toward privacy will change following the Prism issue, according to Brand Republic News. "Issues of privacy, data privacy, data collection, opt-in and the nature of the opt-in and the basis on which it's being made will become more important ... Will young people be unfazed and still disseminate data? I doubt it," he said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00155CKqzOX4d8NwmrN1dopt9RCXtrBOamgtppbBmHckNfnTs6NJVT6HRzfbTtNGCpFjxqPiKS_h-zllC6B8PxY9Ps6H6Rr_EsmEJVooJIZrLlhjCKe83N2yz7sxZgP6ftxaKOJnvvF6HrwWnMdQvGkqGJYmr3QVxlkf-ST8RcJZE1fENcX8em9Mw4VzudUfEODc4jZi6oDfYCJgFfRtsqjvFYu6oXYjVEB9QqrtHCGaQUCa95pEMECrw==> .

Fine, You Can Keep Your Cookie

 

Mozilla is creating a Cookie Clearinghouse in collaboration with the Stanford Center for Internet and Society, according to Ad Age. The clearinghouse would make provisions for companies to issue cookies in special situations -- for example, Facebook's content-delivery domain, fbcdn.net. "Mozilla is joining the advisory board to formulate the process for creating Cookie Clearinghouse allow-lists and block-lists, with the intention of implementing it in Firefox," a Mozilla spokesperson said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t1_IidQzt6XZnirbek2dOL6T-26Mnf0_f4EWWe8o7JG0IU4_NvJJYPJ33eRnF-9_wS8OI7oo2sA8tkn4FO1Uk5lrFfReIgZa6rcZfvIO6X9KAfB6Blk8X1Onf3Bm8ubwG4MIWxoiNO27BfZ6QRmkbgmePGDbjUAhmVwgHGOWMMKFDToLAL2kXuVnO_wHhpA6e8SruzejatjI7XmMJiRibX-> .

 

Shazam The Ratings

 

Do consumers want to "Shazam" ads? Shazam, that little smartphone app that listens to music and tells you what song is playing, is targeting the second-screen trend and rolling out a rating system for measuring TV ad effectiveness. The measurement consists of an ad's Shazam tag volume divided by the gross rating point (licensed from Nielsen). "Consumers have a one-tap, immediate way to get more information, receive special offers, and even shop on the spot with their mobile device ... Advertisers benefit from the direct consumer engagement, and as of today, gain access to insights on the relative performance of their ads airing across television," said Shazam CEO (and former Yahoo executive) Rich Riley in a release. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t2ztzwaeESZ2wdT4QJtKdDdn6u0enfrWnghpkEIJa5cErmRF2LWlONDLvIJLKojlHwAN9toFb6pWKbRKh1Uc31JIRm26ftINiZLBn2jDdUETaUZNSLNIZsELh0piJ7H7tX2yaMZpLD1eVb0_ITqYeoIhxeQAY4qc5iS6l2SDCohqnxJl4HOP2oS> . The proposed TV targeting layer is reminiscent of some things Twitter is doing around TV analytics <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t3wBSL411wxgZEVefxSP-x2usj4vNUpAVm9rD3XP6LRXdhN_qvkf530oZBGtwB9SX9yR0sg6T-Hq066NbqRpHsUrz_fGns7BLQhA8wohEhIev1MXObBF0lowxr6-JtOHNUCu5KvfRQoFG5lOhUko4UeMherY1Yk0i4IBYz6wQuqTLavmkOppkOF9fpn9G0XsqM=> .

 

Marketing The CPA

 

In support of its own efforts to attract global advertisers, Rakuten LinkShare has sponsored a Forrester study about affiliate marketing within eight countries. From the release, a snippet of the findings: "Over the last 12 months, 68 percent of affiliate channel shoppers made an online purchase from a company outside of their home country." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t1DDKoVTkoW5WmAXSHacpBHXIujABLvSrZi3wGSrM4pb20LXYqDhtLF0w2BTk52-Gl6A5qz4ezmLNQNnmhIEAw_MgPRP2gICkomjo2O6BBi3OnZhAS4i5OKuSTdhC5NVQOxXm3o7KJ9Lja9FC87OwwqHp1qquDq6yg=>  And, here's the study (Pay with some PII) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t0VSxPZSyAhxQlrBDmrrJ-rzknzHVF0C2iRAEY4sN72LpniXAklxviyjOQv0jm84j3haN6H9ggmmfUmJjxijM2pW1rtYLFwNM07sUJR8JxszF8817JymrYx2HZOxATLKzJAqCvGkKnA-1uGU3_Q-WQQQAd-eQp7TwMQ9AgdidhEkA==> .

 

Small Biz Boost

 

Advertising accounts for 85% of Facebook's revenue, according to Reuters, and the company announced that it now has 1 million active advertisers on its platform. A lot of that advertising comes from small businesses that take advantage of the reach and frequency Facebook provides. "Most small business owners start off as Facebook users, then migrate to become page owners, and from there migrate to become advertisers," said Dan Levy, Facebook director of small business. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t10CFmXqcw14Oi0AoDShSeXspXcSZnTJ1FJeyif6XAqF-I6-qaptVJTYRoJswYDczTkgQwno0QOHlqCE7rOTYTnQWpjvuvaWlEPncsKH5L14iyl7VsliNNIXQZ23t-5UFte8LKbgjrpejqmDh80-sFIzl9vgRyjlHGEP6XsPnT1_axzSeL2btTfg2Ysnvg_5EdfFnajCwtdJg==> .

 

Funnel Cake

 

Google continues to aim at attribution solutions -- for brands, in particular. Googler Stefan Schnabl announces on the Google Analytics blog that the popular web analytics platform can now "break down the separation between clicks and impressions and give a more complete view of the customer journey. When a user views display ads on the [Google Display Network], or video ads on YouTube, and later visits your website and converts, these interactions with your brand can now be captured in Google. Read about Multi-Channel Funnels. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t2RWSG2-lnnOwoJPE_WQBwUTMkFn1MVTBbSmsI5MLbFXAau0jMKFk-6nnQCbgAJFrscsnLXG5uGwgzuD42tjh7uCFoGlNPdW89jKhHpv7IMhEp3jwAY38HU2451lDXZK-mWlcCpYCT6mO6f8W94KBaxwZcmjWl1K6rBQshWn4P3v6nsYPfIj3KFp-TALYsl9yg=>

Fabulous Millions

 

E-commerce darling Fab.com has raised another $150 million, according to AllThingsD. The company valuation is currently at $1 billion, but CEO Jason Goldberg said, "I don't consider us a success yet ... But we believe in our strategy, and believe it's going to take a good amount of investment to continue to build a 'wow' experience and build a great new e-commerce brand." Of course there are critics who feel the company is growing too fast and won't be sustainable, fearing another Groupon. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t3t3HuRGv_6XcKXpqbHn9HuPfDgLf8jraeKlNRcy73nVDIk5mIhMQEy5UeS-2NBiUn0HVDgzRLyr7qbUzKQcrD3xCDeQ5_Emu0jGSAiwxuJevn9PLyyq_0Ua9XKBTw_1V-jhLLktBHU6no4K-acUcM_gWZNqC0yvhxMdH4DKFs_beXkdUN2W-vexRpDO5Tgl952Ko1kJtzepzE6zgv0RX_-UDxsxXr7vucnoIwBEw-hFHnJkBT5cM_Q9qUOhyBeXkA=> .

 

Picking On The Banner Ad

 

How many times has someone said the banner ad is dead? Yet, as Altimeter Group's Rebecca Lieb points out in an iMedia Connection column, it's still around as a de facto standard. In her own words, "The question isn't whether or not the banner will die. It won't. The question is whether it can lead a more meaningful, rewarding life in the future." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001lNr7TLuj4t1vuy3wMc0O32jEczv40clDhCpkKFY7SUYpwbgS84-QctSFYXG6wxLEx6DmezC1hDDqM1UnuRNXw_WvVT03aYHzHCnuRPYvafly61eLMLVjJ5b2niJ3Uho38X62daaOAVaNa0XdBgePPz0ViBDjDVbb> .

GE Gets Predictive

 

"Predictivity <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj5TLewsMAekncTZ5-Y2eAO3AIJQol2x3OGzNmVW6La_V4bBPqQNQaeDyrgiL48NmelSKUZ5e8LAdCtMpRjxZl049VwA9UwDBpNKzjqN1G3ZLYTajEjGS3S_Ya4W8Oh1xfg=> " -- the name says it all. GE, in partnership with Amazon Web Services, Accenture, and others, are getting into the "big data" and analytics game with a cloud services offering. There's nothing said about ads in the press release, but...listen to the quote from Amazon CTO Werner Vogels in the release: "GE's domain knowledge and R&D capabilities combined with the strength of AWS's global infrastructure, breadth of services and big data expertise will help enable customers to solve problems in ways we haven't even imagined yet, such as improved accuracy in healthcare treatments or extreme levels of energy efficiency." Sounds like good targeting. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj7n4rQ9z9OKAPofuA5Xb8WuoI_A6Vl5zSrmP25A3Nlyvwq3DzUtZotPdJY4JsBzQjzlr8wssLt9DwnQBAo2qs-2r-UY-IZQoJ8TCD0ZYYG06hqX72hDtDQuwlfIt4BqyqVP5RIiu2SrZPg7aNIVFylrzbmm_u6hHEXyY2ZuQwLikSvA_iE524a3VggeLjAABao=> . And, more on All Things D <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj46PWpU47NdThhm7rVfEZyhYq-4aODPX0N03CGPiK-MgJvGPr9_cJAh7RNdkA_pPQS7i32wu0kD_vlQEpW0NfdT5ZYNdh_GXsAiAlPvJgQOIiRnFG642lLwA18BUpwPFauCDx-48892zQg4ByuVfjntkvEBA829Mj7WmtSiELclJQ0sHn3LZySInn7bKHMNHrR4Xnmd5xwRa9RjWEXLboH_9OK0JHya4wBTt20NPd8tgyfmsEZWiCS8b3TsVps1qlJ9TMbk88s4yg==> .

 

Growth Numbers

 

In a quarterly report, ZenithOptimedia Group projects the global ad economy will grow by 3.5% in 2013 rather than the 3.9% they originally reported. According to MediaPost, the U.S. accounts for one-third of all ad spending, followed by smaller and more dynamic markets. ZO Head of Forecasting Jonathan Barnard predicts mobile will grow "five times faster than desktop Internet." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj7Kp_cg-qV9cx7jvqE3EanxxFSE1DLDflpReF_A69Z6SIU26lBdrSrskQQOEEBZpSir6yIjWbAx3t9lhlGyLKmYJicOwTgczvqVikZ5yL_fVk3NVdCZcXNzbIvisjk3BRqh0VvdfyQUbgQBJ8vCERNKrGbIa06yW_7i4AJCaEI7twdpOhClPkhmZ98UlA-_7tKCxXBI9MuUG_DlYIl9ItwoT8NO0VxS5z0Oq30SgiSMKy1dyPVpEAvW> .

 

Ad Tech And The Agency Board Member

 

AdAge takes a look at the conflict of interest created when an agency exec sits on a startup board. TWC's David Kenny and MediaLink's Michael Kassan say such advisory seats are crucial for both parties, but disclosure is a must. "While [Kenny] earned equity from most board positions, he said he never worked with a company that derived more than 1% of its business from his agency." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj6JzGI5O7vzvals8KUGRC8RybqAHp-NoZVIxZknKIFYE_8PX_44sEELiPgc_GTwHhuyCQ-FndTgC53tfGfQOV5EPChCBHHqfPxBDuKjAngOLH2e3SGl4_L4A8dzBIhKya21mw8hUKhqDzMtRwEnUhWenpKOWwEkrSshZLGv3x3VV-KqvCn03cWe8p9ZvFdFnvC8iIjs2pJl3MGbVxkM73nqrnHJ1ZhNN8-tdit-u55Cbg==>  The issue has bubbled up after Tremor's S1 revealed Laura Desmond, CEO of big video spender SMG Global, was granted a whole lot of equity, as observed by the eagle eyes of Stuart Smith <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj47tv5a-EIbKrX6QwPvrQhEXknCpRhKqcelIiDTZ3h2dPRQiDbsMouJ-OawykreAC4GwtsUkQGAXpOUEtPBqFYCSV8v1pPmljMbpE_4OpfyTVl4gVBEDevi-ZuNOT-xEX4NyBPAxSGyOp3Z3Yx_vjc4DzD8n587kXq69jHc3PKkuIALEnwc9aRjR9vNIxi8BlCV8bbN3C55MfcEtPQjtAw9YvIgB1isuBXme4AoLc0W_A==> .

 

Privacy Biz

 

Evidon's business model along with its well-known (in the ad industry) Ghostery plugin are the subject of an MIT Technology Review article. In addition to providing the free Ghostery service that brings transparency to cookies set in browsers across the web, according to MIT Tech, Evidon's revenue-generating products include... : "Companies (...) use Evidon's data to check whether the code they want to deploy is present on every page. The majority of Evidon's analytics customers are large retailers and brands." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj4VNh5-zs49fSvqOvX0ziFneteq8p0I6rS1QZjByqCAhjhqHTbaRVwrCuE72Kka4DvsSwxvic2P93j3PpQ2hkNBbEcXAMjMFOrJU33d1XNBL7buS71LijQtfTylcWwICgH1IRZbF9LjsRa3aFoWii-rPgCgrRVloyoJxDHXQka_kzcdYrFzswb2l5OA_jH3xPCRikZXGO0j8fFMdnqRqV_E> 

 

Party Of The Third Part

 

Mediasmith announced its selection of Medialets for third-party mobile ad serving. Why? A lack of "standards in mobile means that a single campaign's data can leverage different methodologies, making it impossible to effectively gauge success." Hence the need for a third-party ad server, claims the release. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj4QW5_Cyn5Xl4PBGm1vEPNhzO-T_wOG3DeAJsmnAA_gCs6bRNpUyYu44eJxIVGDRqQEDCfUqZ72XWhE823vUMNHspnRZ0sb8JDiK12YWs8PWgt9BeaeUm9z8gLDL4Tt_aDn60fhplfWJ1dNV7Q83-F-cHccicivnsUaDiNNH0ItXxZYD3pVstruModqDvC0ypDBYnj6o0vciQrXyXLDxRFdbxzP3nKYVRN3eSILfk3ciYPiEzFRYEL_e2dEUeZ9uB1c_Bi_MK-pJw==> .

Still More Investing

 

On the heels of WPP Digital's investment in Fullscreen on Monday, WPP Ventures (WPP Digital's progeny) invested in a "Pinterest-like" social media platform called Muzy yesterday. The latest investment round is $4.4 million, angel-backed by Marc Andreessen and Ben Horowitz. The social media site has about 20 million users and is adding 1 million a month, according to TechCrunch. Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj6d8KASX2-BuC9brIj-tziD8VYk5-cY4bMBKChbrXYR5VBPIP3mBIW64_8Nrt2_uE64OHyg3HniMp3JnUKtjZHRr3EveIO3tYysLOWDXyYzC2iluJvIyY2WpZKoXUrtdSFbC4m_ywxzICA2CYp42iHYfcBF5lBC7tuueTC-1jRvQXXY8s7P7kttbBiwonynhrfamerCokbVgUkQQupT5ftv75LM95kw3vjUsxU6Qh_c6Q==>  That's a lotta logins.

 

Mobile Ads Worth More -- To Facebook

 

Facebook charges more money for mobile ads than desktop, the opposite of what most ad platforms do, according to Social News Daily. Mobile still only accounts for 2% of all company ad budgets and CPMs are typically much lower on mobile than desktop. However, consumer trends say you'd better be ready for mobile, Ms. Or Mr. Publisher. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj7bS8P6wjKY1FXzd2Cj3NhP-Trq4xhfLlj8SfN_cVzdEA33mpMwIbDq88kif0QSO_KqD-a1BfrJTz77q7kRunIGN1DwD8XhJ_t76h049RkVu-YBKHjEhVPa80mXcUDhb5bOENldeMKBpkKX_M3h7O_lZvwdGBeKewjZC0FFBjOlZebInXSkkfoCs75my7UTWWbot7dZ_zNdqjrxOU9dKo4N> .

 

Data Race

 

Salesforce has gotten a leg up in the race to dominate the marketing data market after its ExactTarget acquisition, according to AdAge's Travis May. Although they are up against other major players like Merkle and Adobe, there is still a large amount of fragmentation in the data-management space. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj4_N4edFph4ChGVu0g8T28fuex3PyGzyRIE92zJErLlRRuUAzSLX2RVFbmK1xlbiJTmUjM5dV-F4WVFcPvQduANWglB8YZljo8VLjSrHz5CiYT3m9mgTa8GAkxmtbEL5tqADNQ573AlLkvQxP-vIhRlniXohzTzCKIybRSLHv6fPJAZni2Gh4ekyG4JjlPgh5sBDoyhcVjmUunsSey3OvcJVWkvM_D4n28=> .

 

Dynamic Microsoft

 

Microsoft is getting creative with its ad offerings for Windows 8 apps. According to a Microsoft blog post, "Nearly 60% of people exposed to ads on Windows 8 perceived the brands as innovative. cutting edge and trustworthy." Device Idea

 

Sell-side platform PubMatic announced last week that's it's using a combination of AdTruth and TrustE to provide targeting other than the cookie-based variety. The company said it will talk more about the solution in a panel discussion <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj5XHKsSvsHVg4AlTRFanAh1rJxIu7kenSnm9A8Icoc6EHi1F66jfTB-JV4urKniGvvC4Y9OO7eypP1_GeVhbNfdQrcZ1G4-lPA2OklopDBDi9tcQTiR7UVyDbXiMLVtqb97G4Z--iGh2dgWjzi_lhhEcaDSuYjhfp_jnrJMThHDF9I9LEKPJ43ic8V_gZpY8Ls=>  at Cannes. Yield And The Paywall

 

As yield lovers well know, the cost of renewals is incredibly important for subscription services, and Scout Analytics (AdExchanger Q <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj647Nc97SOaJwKioXbixukJzPmmf8hqr2llvgpc3FX6DVX9mMzH1qMipXMCoLbpkmQfaLH9DrHYNNee6-YLwXG7S_rRnr9tgjtPHREA3YY18FTdL-Lly0DSknuYnuTgfDDzL-jCM8cE63x3eD-wVck6UkzHjyngkVsqafWKJN-VjUT8lDzrAmJhVgt2FjpNI8snaNs0-Shjqg==> &A, April 2013) has developed a calculator as part of its Renewal Performance Management solution. The calculator gives companies an idea of what they need to break even -- and also the potential for revenue. The calculator is here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj4Nojz7mopn2lWREBOcIPEvuoSMOzANdRTu9x4xBDsBWsSTij-LIPl7uoMygw8S9yO7KtyYMkex_HlSwyRb3cibyvGYEn63KjoCVGTTZgTX5QE9FigH7Cm575KcwjGMqnumA4EylG2gKUbP_I6egAXB> , and the press release from earlier this month is here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001tKeBDO4ZRj5FWDrkzazhYZayXwY05n4dTMod0GS2W1qSO43Jdcp5q3GNGpA9vv6neCZiZR16lhTVausOXETU1kb10UlNJbV6vGSTpLKqQQwt8k_MczSkp_CFDhSByLQmaWi7NiWTrgk6MO4uC3-4z72U05CkW8Hi4I6-XiBCEANR5Z3xwcb73Q==> .

 In The Comments <http://ih.constantcontact.com/fs116/1102602719219/img/119.png>  

 

From "At What Price Safety? At What Price Targeted Advertising?"...

*	Ramsey McGrory, AddThis: "I'm not sure what Jim is advocating here....other than saying, 'go ahead and block 3rd party cookies and allow DNT.' 

*	If the argument is that we're just not being transparent enough, I'd like to understand what defines sufficiently transparent. The IAB, DAA and others have served billions of ads educating consumers. 
*	Users understand how to clear cookies and often do when they don't want activity to be tracked. On some sites, anywhere from 10-80% of activity is being cleared.
*	Cookies are anonymous, generally standardized technology and the alternatives may end up being more invasive. 
*	Many pixels or cookies that a user sees are not directly collecting data for OBA. Transparency and context is needed here without fear mongering..." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016MmWTJMuNeqBF8Tl9geMfIgbGuBuin96Y1u4w1cliYZaU-8A7wFSkdKOkzRco3KztVfqV78oVNOmUlhblRZ4YR8JtTtg23HfrPXvgOqxUzVs7fS-2u_pBLlYCJx1x4sgwqpV16PkpgvJJ-rWbQ0CABlL_GzTAviwd7vMe2PHH_4N846DFn2oiUgTZX6KA15hnF7fesT2TlYody4Ek9ZQUtk4YLGi18skIjKPOoblkeBiQCec1rXOOQ==> .

Agency Investment

 

WPP has invested in Fullscreen, a network of YouTube channels, as part of a reported 8-figure venture capital round. The LA Times quotes Fullscreen CEO George Strompolos, "We feel that the media company of the future ultimately won't be built on a satellite in the sky, it'll be built on software. There's so much we can do to empower this next generation of creators." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016MmWTJMuNeoKw_db79pY244fzgdV3kZgcXLDvNt4deIyHWVPK0BF12Ik-yblUYRT43PuL5f8WXFbUHMsMGqPvQeNhhBilpJP6a1V2K2tM0f80eVmx0POwUsyqRpD76-x4uS264zCT7evk-7ks1677DSFvYrqUK5WM51fFSZpEeagdNp4M8olK8Cld1kDFwCIHX3NyKRP-DEBNVccWDqLow==> .

Its latest is with Mass Relevance (AdExchanger Q <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016MmWTJMuNeq8CGC0XMu0ggdPT9YZmzQ_O40snbARbpfFpqbPSp7EVVGADFCeS44j1lfBWrF8G5Bkfa8NcfIVkH014ZUXW3Nq7m4-1TJGWqVLwzZGrIwiGfvwFlj6AeouRHmxfCZL4_uQqDBzPZdNTrgfhZm-mMkif6ySVNpY7YAQAPRVR70uo7qbW26GsRQ7Df1ieb9RhFybuMaQn6REQq9HsDL4O_Jp6_TURaypF2sj6LTTlYXIdQ==> &A from May) to "create and integrate social media experiences on client-maintained properties across any digital device and surface," according to a press release. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016MmWTJMuNer8_aFpd_gAFlStXZLt2AFQYsJRzd0J-amLzFBBUG6g5AL2CdsfCFCykPcNvd2sU1uVSWIVJ4YPc3vpUf_HLVIW6uo8CQZqtwfTMYiS_3mjzzf3_C-a9b32i55S8RARPe-QogtxofQ11wglTldi4Yg-n7UXgdIeLJt-Frs5J1btSckYNq3RK9fxS1meZiIKuOwvZXh6sygvwaUu_9DQnc70hOgLJJo_H5icsJY-x7F4rxCIfpJwHRjB> . Click Love

 

Yesterday, Facebook announced that it is making its ads even more click-friendly. From the Facebook Studio blog, "Facebook Page post link ads are optimized to drive off-site conversions and sales. Over the past several months, aligned with updates to News Feed, we've enlarged images and the clickable area for Page post link ads on both desktop and mobile." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016MmWTJMuNeqChwLdqa3QA4uz93OsUzAb6_g9FWVJDmQtV8aXZVXRLFwNdiEQXMmWxv-KeCp0v0OTwXX-FIopq4rnn_CIR1z3NF8gwSKMDgGkhzbJEGfYXo6bP3K1rK5cr0K_FjPfcNDFPOXs9PGnp5uebkRoXkXMXH8Ccc6UA4JRwCBQbwhgYvtLjLE-xT1TRfhuAYAWWYkGk4HN7ka45A==> 

 

Get Rewards

 

A study conducted by Millward Brown revealed consumers engage more with ads that provide rewards. "Schwa!?" Also in the study, consumers prefer to have control over the incentives rather than being surprised. "Schwa!? Schwa!?" "Mobile advertising experiences that create a more balanced consumer experience -- ones that respect time and provide a useful outcome -- open the door of receptivity and have a positive impact on the brand," said Jayne Dow, a researcher at Firefly, Millward Brown's global qualitative practice. Apple And The NSA

 

Apple wants you to know your information is mostly safe with them, according to a post on its site. "Regardless of the circumstances, our Legal team conducts an evaluation of each [U.S. government] request and, only if appropriate, we retrieve and deliver the narrowest possible set of information to the authorities." The company says information from iMessage, FaceTime, Map searches and Siri searches are never collected and therefore can't be disclosed to law enforcement or the government. What Brian Believes

 

AppNexus CEO Brian O'Kelley believes in the future of journalism, maybe not in print form, but definitely digitally and funded by ads, according to The Guardian. "The amount of quality supply [of content] online isn't growing, while I think that advertising interest in it is going to grow significantly, and we'll see CPMs [cost per 1,000 impressions] increase rapidly over the next few years," O'Kelley said. MRC Updating 'Viewability'

 

The Media Rating Council released an update on their efforts to solve the viewability issues of online advertising. Next month advertisers can expect to see a draft version of guidelines for measuring viewable impressions, followed by a report identifying the "discrepancies" between vendor solutions later this year, according to David Gunzerath, SVP and associate director of the MRC. "We're out there auditing and accrediting companies and...honing in on where the differences are occurring and hopefully shedding some light on this issue," Gunzerath said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ODFzCzl8A41nMTo2M5xakMx9xXCG_DtFmH11tHwNCOt_m-XQaOzP3l31R_SPrgqpYonYakFnMu7o_tnBYVqs3M_raq88ALtS3ejsnjGV0ri4lrqS2_l5DqYYY97rnx_8fgcMEXqarN-GC7u3rramHnH4TNHJ3z1gh-2biPRYvK15O1ZUdIpA5zfzDd8mxe2YwL2HUdQpA4w4yeD0IV6sBa3cjo_lAIGIg9ho14HHfJ4=> .

 

Google Consolidating Mediation

 

Google continues to consolidate its ad products and the latest to get the axe is its AdWhirl mobile advertising platform, which is part of AdMob. The shutdown will take effect on September 30, according to TechCrunch, leaving mobile developers scrambling to migrate to a new platform. A letter to AdWhirl users states: "The open source code for AdWhirl will still be available if anyone wants to run their own AdWhirl service...We encourage you to start using AdMob Mediation prior to 30 September." Read more on TechCrunch <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ODFzCzl8A42DgN7f0DkgW7tOJzC6fMWyKpzDAhxmlQtEVdbA8QPheduvgNz-aTQG_HbjQxeZMYgP0r6BGnfuizW5AhPfqKrCRp9JILGGwf3-D-adyprt_JCWlvVbAxPjdNZ5nfomIuYDjdXDjd0bt-t8kJ0QE-GiHTFe6UqeBJjONs3CF7ss64HfJ1nHngQLwlc7DaCBVLjgreFjandWX35T-NM-B-bnW9uBF82Vj7nd2Ft77TTdiqYhJmHzR-HwhhBpms0zFiU=> .

 

Cannes Tech

 

The annual global advertising event known most simply as "Cannes" is going full-throttle this week. The Wall Street Journal notes the throngs including ad platform firm Turn's presence and quotes thusly: "'We signed some contracts with contacts we made during our first time at Cannes last year, so this year we decided to step up our presence,' said Jean-Claude Muratore, who heads up the French business of Turn." Read more (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ODFzCzl8A40SylAUy5FUxwMN1PFX7kEPTQ22W2yQMwzbmY11eG07VrlsNhapdCg78cg9ot5cb9OlBWX9NNZJ9m61sC2rWRum3Epuuqt3ogMjt1FtuMGG6QVDQFUSMAb2V1D9Vp6Mt29KYxb5APqy6BaWIYbEu7JNfHVM48cbyI08O6cuhvVRbhG4SjD6UOUY> . And, visit the Cannes Lions site. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ODFzCzl8A41R9B3uZIXTHU-IqqMLSp9Pp1cNbYbJOsy58h5tF4JIUbKmrZ_lnne7NY7RCDEDlYdWPoDhEvjlu_WRze5y5F7qbuVL63F2iDFYqdiMv62unf6KAL6-bpOl> 

 

Sponsored Yield

 

On Digiday, Josh Sternberg covers pricing for sponsored content products across publishers. For Buzzfeed he finds, "$100,000 gets four or five listicles, sorry posts, created by Buzzfeed's in-house creative services team. Although some buyers said they've gotten posts for as little as $5,000 with a minimum spend of $50,000." Nice yield. And the ROI?... Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ODFzCzl8A43p4iVikhiWg_dr9tOiNOZJphocrrp7HihRWbYhrQTHMVnAqD9s-0iS7InoHmxOmEb15joIkb6D1kGc2BNNGJWKPjYzXFKdWtTUQNxwbYClkUxKm1wVehBzINx9l95HZAgO1-6odLs1WbtqKdqKKsdpA-Ac-JV53b1NtGI0q1UJjgCNU-lxbVV5WFEPM4jfgJc=> 

 

Self-Regulation And The NSA

 

Skip Graham, Digital Net Agency's Chief Strategy Officer, expressed his concern that consumers are more complicit with PRISM because of the work advertisers did to convince them data collection was acceptable, according to ZDNet. "We went first and told the public not to worry, to have faith and to trust. We crafted the arguments, molded the opinions, and quieted the skeptics...We convinced the public it was safe, and that self-regulation and not legislation was the answer. The NSA and the current administration is making the same argument now," said Graham. On B2B Marketers

 

eMarketer's Noah Elkin spoke with Google's Mike Miller about trends in digital business-to-business marketing. Miller said, "We still see a very strong orientation around search. We see some customers using display advertising and some moving into social, although they're still trying to figure some of that out. We've also seen some customers starting to make use of video platforms. For us, that's YouTube. Mobile is also a theme, although that cuts across each of those platforms." Mobile Giants

 

Google captured $4.6 billion in mobile ad revenue last year, fully half the global spend, according to eMarketer. Facebook, who just began mobile advertising in 2012, is expected to increase mobile ad revenue by 333% this year. And Twitter, Pandora and YP are each carving out a small but measurable piece of the pie. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVawimITx83Q0cEw2et5R8sSIdSr4w87O-7lbhvj5VLCBW1do07Pstm45K2fmfVSqVUoUjQp-JRQIb-bsWHQm-fGtUA-_iYC-Op0MFnAT6q49wVnOVxVCLi_YAGLE-62el1_cRYDG8ifUNaukj8P98NQW5IOHzxnBSjv_bITmQV3xV8c730Q_WQR69U2h51VqH80HKoixp-rAZ65zCPJ09Gt8WpBBMixM37I=> .

 

Twitter's Quiet Analytics Rollout

 

Chris Penn, VP of Marketing Technology at SHIFT Communications, writes about Twitter's new, yet unpublicized, analytics tools. "The data you get is fairly thin. You get follow and unfollow counts over the last 3 days, you get mentions, and then you get the ability to see Favorites, Retweets, and Replies." There's no official yet from Twitter, according to The Next Web <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVawWaojcnkvVo_WytaYMDgysXR6hvsduCQqKpCbZ_DsJTWst14wk2-7Dbc8N3_zYOgSwQ57nsv6AUhOAHQ70u3gvNJqei8Oyvh2xxfwMlUvo0UnJ7SNH4JtT5TLxn0Cu52dVEwfCUuvT0--sQo4VyHwKCCchYXLY1Ov0jWPj6ClCqRMrBeatZBEpbwEf03cd-KTa0CIWkjd5XvQpw3lmpfJjDnXk8xA9s696owIHlhqCBE30qnWVK01kdCgRqOFpCjDxVF-NanljPzONaN8pXtrH>  and Marketing Land <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVayL40edTKI6hg6HGNCu1YZa5Uq7fMgDYtILTWenMTrNm4LovfB3GWaNANELY_hC2Ld-aNQ97_LsHPFsxzty2IISU7RZwvfPC3UH1klqXPxWEjMvLsileh2Ds9tOsQNUsRm65PY2x08DSdevOC1xWNbcGlNyR2NZ3eU9Dc794GsV10Y0jLfGe3GWTCOIncaqjdOHfksLYyXo7RQuJy6ALAJw> , who also covered the story. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVaxGjkrBi1caKXbBo9sAucgErBA_q40tbQsnF-a0Vr6ZfpjWTprZs7ExG1_BGIotN2TLT8dzUz-AVDggzdfKdykkEn2G4h9UhJwmQegrsgCwvcOxmZwSaMVEyK7LHKYTu4EUGPwIvmshL9J5_TuOfQumcA-KouqbYpfvK7HPDT-E0tVm9CWrNKlh1gdOEDFtQvzkxFTvpT3j8Q==> .

 

Offline CRM Gets Data-Driven

 

A LiveRamp and myThings partnership will bring offline CRM data to display ad campaigns. "This integration empowers data-driven marketers to personalize advertising offerings using their CRM data across all marketing channels and funnels," said Auren Hoffman, CEO of LiveRamp. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVaxVUEawCeook6_ZA91zvxDLrJZxF2fDxZI8SAUdjjyD2yqCPuxupbbAnYEtZ7QL5UAtIRwi7KQMXfvJgg4cTh9umELkCS8sZAkuzmOVgwCo5S-ehVCi7QLhGFSQ5hBBgRE8s8Yp4DhARWwrD12vK1G5IQtrrRmh1ZkkqCjDHQmkh6sVrnJghjig2jfJ6LuNydyCBnicdSlZgfdGS83vRvF8Ak64OoR2hmzpIZvMHSnNLnZtp6OmOv52sMj7pamKZU8fiiYVfHNbPG5LWElORG_Q> .

 

Don't Forget Myspace

 

Myspace still exists, and it hopes television commercials will remind people of that fact. The 90-second commercial, which can be found on AdAge, features big name celebrities and will begin airing in 30-second clips starting tonight. This is part of a $20 million campaign spearheaded by Specific Media, which acquired Myspace in 2011. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVayoypnDYGUozKtFp5pDMMnkxetPgADqcbDXlw_boqZxKyIzOtW1uiFFKpDzv45pb1V1Ogv5M1IT2OkoOq3zowf1ThcO0My1DagNrxmoUPE0jk5KWdA4xSwRLlFF5_QQzi_r8xstt8ZrculvJi9R10r-JzDWgnE3-AKuHxAn7ONwNTy6X4eZfhIc> .

 

Amobee Goes Out-Of-Home

 

Amobee is branching out into digital-out-of-home in Asia, where there is an increasing amount of money in retail and mobile, ZDNet is reporting. Amobee was acquired by Singapore based telco SingTel last year. Their DOOH platform ties in to mobile as well, for example in shopping malls, where they encourage shoppers to interact with both in-store screens and then their own mobile phones. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ex1jHRpaVayIkCbjwJEkoj581BgS_DM3x3tE5hdj1dIZue4gxOjYJZJDV5sJT8g3DklBe-9q39xMVmS4_8VzN56IrId76VZTaw5Z4i53Acz1FcdKLLMzYdECZ3X_dU7b0viTGbmYScFSIjwotLCEzyHQRuzDuGr-i1B6tlGUXSdCvwGcI1NoLiH_sHNyPSpJU4hplYgUGabeFRzgd3T9lA==> .

Facebook Bags Hashtags

 

Facebook is co-opting some of Twitter's real-time cred with the addition of hashtag support for users and brands. In a blog post, it suggests marketers can stop worrying about going "all in" with Twitter when launching hashtag-based campaigns in their billboard or TV creative: "If you are already using hashtags in an advertising campaign through other channels, you can amplify these campaigns by including your hashtags in Facebook advertising." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgyGgFJpawSHnXXjmHkpDMe99toNHCTbGM_ad9p5IJwoK1hIL45jQNInpgeMVNjZlW218lV00Il0-W9uIkMUBixC2lekcaKGxZVC_gFLJMVG7CnnvTKCTrNmel8MCOw1cxTbx29z__4MXuhshzxWFno7nuhCfOrAExe3kzE66-zqGBVgZUQh9Gno>  Long-term, the hashtag idea could serve as the foundation of an exchange linking ads to trending ideas or big news. Read AdExchanger's recent speculations <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgzk5Y8TBZ-l9-NdcrUB7e0HFTU0kSJ81Zu-h1yPEGJFZOfLOJOOnaWUAB7lgTjjEy1irPOcqAV_9Iop83TlS4F5LnuK_n-g-VO_ZFNXjiI2TdOaOfJ6MWnN9I1cuqfOtMxOe1tKeeYfJ6mN4-cjTNYbZNquu5P4Dc2UCjxjM9gD5uL1ULlM7lvl> .

 

AdRoll Buys Data Miner

 

Retargeter AdRoll has snatched up two-man data-crunching firm Bitdeli. Bitdeli was created by two brothers, Jyri and Ville Tuulos, to support custom analytics. Ville built framework and Jyri is the design guy. Founded last year, "Bitdeli quickly signed up hundreds of developers onto the platform, and is processing hundreds of millions of events in real time. The challenges of crunching, analyzing, and presenting these massive data sets are similar to that of the retargeting space," says a press release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgylNdp44r_ffEVcgqCluDGucUMoSV5ANjkRq21qr0BJBD-yzHQlMRMrkITE5Ur090qFDMzar4NQFge8eueO7MO0kKKkCIIkGv2dB6ETmnLJrAk-dFWFB9p8GGhh2704haRmer7I_PQlnHSjPgJJQ9N_zikRWHTgO3evpx2-xDVbrniWSZM8T1Gup5my5JASxvh6fGqc25wcm4pgIUtyn8Zu> . AdRoll blog <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgyraWJ-MpTMHKAosRzF0QnerbYWyF44XtVD2eInoOM5LcvTdWp1LMu5728SXAOOOzEKFsTRj2dymXw6bqike-qGt75FEZrl0EVS01sxx2WP-dXVVW8zkjkikvc-6_tfwplPoI5cH_N3HQ==> .

 

Another Publisher Goes Native

 

If you had any doubt that native advertising was really happening, think again. The Washington Post is joining the long list of other publishers taking on this ad format. Their ads are called "Sponsored Views" and, according to AllThingsD, they are positioned at the very bottom of the page. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgzLDaoCjKvnxRvg6x7UrmkAiqTkNuaeJ634AyUfIghd8fEP-sw8ddihEdsCCuoQnjz6Oakn_R-4RDBr7_clfOhgmCPc9GD19qmK6CFKx8YQM1pLd2B3ag_du7JahFgm4VUch2-Y3ad165iHtfGgfAmsBW-67MjspM3SMtBnszsoo4GvvAipI_je4nPUIpRlDL8=> .

 

Flite Takes Off

 

Real-time ad company Flite raised $9 million from Iris Capital. Part of the deal includes VivaKi's use of the technology across Publicis Groupe's agencies, according to a press release. Recent acquisitions of similar companies were quite bullish (Buddy Media for $745m and Vitrue for $300m). Flite is in an even better strategic position in the market of paid media publishing. "This market is still in its infancy, with potential to be massive," said Rishad Tobaccowala, Chief Strategy and Innovation Officer of VivaKi. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgx0JwiH8OsdZA0hAREn_6J-mt-lZ2ibCffzP0sGg4DQDWAN9OLvbMDM18dqXalZbAMc_e1T6Cg8O2AI9J3ArHc7xHNnR7ANaEnyy29-od9Gs0zRA1bIt6-eJk24BggGWRTKYKQfDhlqcniXrC_kp8zhlE9ctNsMxijlJDbvpEsiv8KNKPaKY95Z-6QD8uo-SwqMU0RMshZ4OQDKKOOja8AjaIJZJHeuqLt-5Aa747oRhkpuAVyvYJYN_GazhgWvtKk_zj74a7MZsA==> .

 

What Is Your Info Worth?

 

The NSA data collection scandal has a lot of people in a tizzy, but what about advertisers who do the same thing for profit? The Financial Times took the trouble to break out just how much money your data is worth, unveiling the financial side of data collection. The minimum per person is around $0.0005, but that number goes all the way up to $0.001 for income and shopping histories. Furthermore, although health information is supposed to be protected, companies get around that by saying their data is from patients themselves and not a larger database. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgy1kgkJ10tAD6awHnJrFRq4ehqD_ulCkMaKsxMrT2cJba98RN_wBcMgjiNIj-___UCsJ4rXPgC2J3xR7ZS3boEb_6mur78DJwE8g0v7YPI65u8VmWUx5YdfUJ7Dw4lZv3gp8ZCw4bh64DiEBdp6BcITEOb0RtXRCoUM5lUYUBTZTX28-58A8l9pQHOORfjxVWQ=> .

iAd Opens Up

 

Apple is opening up their iAd platform to smaller developers with the iAd Workbench platform, lowering the purchase minimum to $50 rather than the cool million it was reportedly charging big brands a few years ago. According to GigaOM, the ads are in banner format and appear at the top of apps, giving developers multiple targeting and pricing options. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgz4KaATcpl1fG-BD1-4_NUfY2nRKZx4xysi25QeX9tgK99Dhp_o98vPitIxMCgN9gyId3serO6OeMzVIfXC9fIdn6ph8QVB5N58JKgM6ULQSw7V63-JA6K0RbYXdHKuuEgFYVvYNyA98xa5gWadDE9YGRztsTfbWi4sK0KID3nOroeHqHn42CupORTWXeN9qnPzBd7xUm6FtwAqNM_u83EG_AF48-1spqg=> .

 

Digital Cars

 

The automotive industry is expected to be the second biggest spender in online advertising by 2015, according to eMarketer. Also, according to the National Automobile Dealers Association, dealers have increased their digital ad spending from 5.0% in 2002 to 26.5% in 2012. It seems the auto industry has used digital advertising to change consumer habits from the traditional purchase funnel to a more cyclical process, a trend which was explored in a report from 2012 done by Google, Compete and R.L. Polk. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001zv7M9-usfgwIu9aPBQxqu2vgYsrEGwr9rre8x2XR_Fafz_Dsy9_bOd4rXCt89EbGp5XlD1bYE-icMFRb4UPj4SPxwho3zwxHoSIDVOJCmkuSYA88k_t6TWub97FsGr49NGjjvD37Qn8s-jdji9ZMplbjzgy7x4Ts9sv1_UTT_Uwq6ZuU1NJHBEzhzIBAtIxnpsu41f3HVsyKt4tCESQ_0KbgE9kDiim8xUK8jN00CBQ=> .

Spreading Viewability

 

comScore was spreading its viewability mantra across the media yesterday. The Wall Street Journal's Suzanne Vranica covers the industry conundrum and finds a marketer who is making demands. She writes, "ConAgra is now demanding that all its display-ads deals come with some sort of guarantee from publishers that their ads will be visible to the human eye and/or its online video, and display ads will be seen by a bigger swath of its target audience. [Heather Dumford of ConAgra] said ConAgra will make sure that a Web publisher runs ads as many times as it needs to ensure that it gets the correct amount of viewable ads it has paid for." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ECxJK0NT2EyL_u3QRmU9T91BT61Y05F0FKeosOmOAKo43zi9wOGe7u5lqGVjof35kE9vcL66Ao16MRH-GZCItTB-SVx8IDnEP08wzumW87vV572n6ZRi6BjNKrIJGKcbVi3sFqUN2ndfWH-ABKraPwtUrBn1JQgfbUJ9AqcEfUfEPN6Swl7y-xaMwRMxGO_s> . Meanwhile, Ad Age has a viewable story with quotes from Kellogg's, among others. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ECxJK0NT2Ey0FbtnldNX5jqCHh67jeW5YKlJcqS_wEnRF8FGusPKHsHhj3CaqCpXv8x3FG525kVs2MAUPxT36HJ0on36hypvZmAUJyVHuCzKno-tlbv6pnRN0epNPXPWPfZN1xR4LxuwSi2PHmouyyh6_zA96zqOgGayKRey0zTnX6guxhCqwHbVm7Lootwo> 

 

Marketo Says Tweet

 

Marketo is launching a new product called Customer Engagement Marketing, which uses algorithms to generate messages for customers based on behavior. According to PCWorld, the product also uses cookies, buttons and other technology to avoid spamming someone with the same message. By applying machine learning to social messages, Marketo hopes they reach the consumers most likely to take action. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ECxJK0NT2Ew9dFL1P7mnsE16-zUqfXk5qa1sN_Vf38t1Mp3nlNMXudPzhmhA4o9Bb4J1k93ejDaOCDi2KqOUsc4DWeVETkQhyTGtQk3nvDtS9l3XlWOprzTgdB4oAECsPX7e-RmoWQzyvQiDmffaWAouPL1SE-Jsz7btnOYqi1peoikr1JOIHoWQQShjgVI2dHo8YFp7dBjqUQEwtRnktwsCsFUb9xcF0iYjyJ9gQOufRfCas3svqw==> .

 

Desktop Ads Are Doomed

 

Soon mobile will no longer be optional, at least according to eMarketer, as desktop ad spending will peak in 2014 and then begin to decline thereafter. Mobile, however, will continue growing at staggering rates, if their reports are accurate. Digital video and sponsorships appear to be the only desktop formats that won't stagnate or decline. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ECxJK0NT2EynE1JSC1q5YuZGog3WFmH_sKPp8vGFwxqRIMu7menp5YGpT14K4fNHMlqxRl4qYAN_EXRbFdrf-l_aBVsYxK75BXHmlKMF8eGcrMRSb65e_31L5bry19QjibmvtCgKOJg740GRBnsBeCqRqTiIPlESRqrsbiq9ZEaODAnuBtDH9Kz92iuZhoxu> .

 

Local, Mobile, Ads

 

There's no denying mobile is growing, but local mobile advertising is growing at different rates depending on the market. Overall, local mobile advertising will double this year, according to Borrell, from $1.5 billion to $3.2 billion. StreetFight rounds out Borrell's figures, saying, "Last year, mobile ads accounted for 8% of the $18.5 billion spent on local online advertising. This year's growth will put its share at 13% of $24.3 billion." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ECxJK0NT2EwuQgqWDMuQvLlBBEzyQjPcMok5NEEbJqBgrwhbra2u3BOFScZd9VIUiOI6EqqkMPgz0GOMWQXiufgbJI2OOl72vLb8W88VDR68lXHv6W31m0DGvYuy0hmKw_L29DipagHDUYklwjY67lnlqcSn68JccDc4Od7jl1tSy9HO2CrcAN2o_6yXxw7ADOIMhppVLAG9bZ097zJ3jbnDl2igByDZZyOYI91d-jY=> .

 

Mobile Retargeting

 

Another player has popped into the mobile retargeting space as TechCrunch's Anthony Ha reports that former Pontiflex VP of mobile Brian Long is the CEO and co-founder of TapCommerce. His company has some "secret sauce" tech which allows TapCommerce to retarget in the targeting-deprived mobile environment. Ha adds, "In addition to its retargeting technology, the company says it has developed dynamic ad units and audience segmentation tools." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ECxJK0NT2EyZHey03LAsg-jOSNtyDjSw6IOKjGZXLzH_0uQJYOZn4g-hRzus0jBoLoknGojj01jrFcJX1UV9iwx-fFBc-QnACRnkpKtrXoRXeY8YHayi-aRBIztFb6We5Ome36J1nnBVpgeLxsHDBNpNX3jLXibvlR7j-0WYr0o=> .

*	Amit Avner, CEO, Taykey: "The impact for streamlined ad formats will be that there is more thought put into the limited formats, which I believe will result in partners innovating on the existing formats." 
*	Don Mathis, CEO, Kinetic Social: "Facebook's recent moves bode well for PMDs that focus on advanced delivery technologies... but not so much if a PMD's value-add is limited to decrypting the (increasingly straight-forward) Facebook ad platform."
